I plan to come to this hotel again in winter to see the Siberian swans.

msg:An old five-star hotel in Shanzhou Park. Nearby are the Sanmenxia Museum, Bell and Drum Tower, etc., with an excellent geographical location. The hotel has three buildings, courtyard-style buildings, because it is in the park, there are many ancient trees, and the environment is elegant. The buffet dinner is 88 yuan per person, with good variety and appearance, and high cost performance. It is very close to the Yellow River, convenient for watching swans. It is close to Pier 1 and you can take a sightseeing boat. The pick-up station is a major feature, thumbs up. The drawback is that the occupancy rate is high and there are too many people for breakfast. The check-in and cleaning are slow, and I didn't get into the room until 3 pm.
